class VideoAIEditor {
  // 1. Video Generation (ØªÙˆÙ„ÙŠØ¯ ÙÙŠØ¯ÙŠÙˆ Ù…Ù† Ù†Øµ)
  async textToVideo(script: string) {
    // Runway ML API
    return await runwayml.generate({
      prompt: script,
      duration: 30,
      resolution: "1080p"
    });
  }
  
  // 2. Auto Video Editing (Ù…ÙˆÙ†ØªØ§Ø¬ ØªÙ„Ù‚Ø§Ø¦ÙŠ)
  async autoEdit(videoFile: File) {
    // Descript API
    return await descript.edit({
      file: videoFile,
      actions: [
        "remove_silence",
        "add_captions",
        "remove_filler_words", // "Ø£Ù…Ù…Ù…", "ÙŠØ¹Ù†ÙŠ"
        "color_correction"
      ]
    });
  }
  
  // 3. AI Avatar (Ø´Ø®ØµÙŠØ© AI ØªØªÙƒÙ„Ù…)
  async createAIAvatar(text: string, voice: string) {
    // HeyGen API
    return await heygen.generate({
      script: text,
      voice: voice,
      avatar: "professional_male_arabic"
    });
  }
  
  // 4. Auto Subtitles (ØªØ±Ø¬Ù…Ø© ØªÙ„Ù‚Ø§Ø¦ÙŠØ©)
  async addSubtitles(videoFile: File, language: string) {
    // OpenAI Whisper
    const transcript = await openai.audio.transcriptions.create({
      file: videoFile,
      model: "whisper-1"
    });
    
    // ØªØ±Ø¬Ù…Ø©
    const translated = await openai.chat.completions.create({
      model: "gpt-4o",
      messages: [{
        role: "user",
        content: `Translate to ${language}: ${transcript.text}`
      }]
    });
    
    return { transcript, translated };
  }
  
  // 5. Video Upscaling (ØªØ­Ø³ÙŠÙ† Ø§Ù„Ø¬ÙˆØ¯Ø©)
  async upscaleVideo(videoFile: File) {
    // Topaz Video AI
    return await topaz.upscale({
      file: videoFile,
      targetResolution: "4K",
      fps: 60
    });
  }
}

class ElementorAI {
  // 1. ØªØ­Ù„ÙŠÙ„ ØªØµÙ…ÙŠÙ… Elementor
  async analyzeElementorDesign(elementorJSON: any) {
    // Elementor Ø¨ÙŠØ­ÙØ¸ Ø§Ù„ØªØµÙ…ÙŠÙ… ÙƒÙ€ JSON
    const sections = elementorJSON.content;
    
    return {
      layout: this.extractLayout(sections),
      colors: this.extractColors(sections),
      typography: this.extractTypography(sections),
      widgets: this.extractWidgets(sections)
    };
  }
  
  // 2. ØªÙˆÙ„ÙŠØ¯ ØªØµÙ…ÙŠÙ… Elementor Ù…Ù† Ø§Ù„ØµÙØ±
  async generateElementorDesign(prompt: string) {
    // Ø§Ø³ØªØ®Ø¯Ø§Ù… O3 Ù„ØªÙˆÙ„ÙŠØ¯ Ø§Ù„Ù‡ÙŠÙƒÙ„
    const design = await openai.chat.completions.create({
      model: "o3-mini",
      messages: [{
        role: "system",
        content: `Ø£Ù†Øª Elementor Pro Expert.
        
        Ø³ØªØªÙ„Ù‚Ù‰ ÙˆØµÙ Ù„Ù…ÙˆÙ‚Ø¹ ÙˆÙŠØ¨ØŒ ÙˆØ¹Ù„ÙŠÙƒ Ø¥Ù†Ø´Ø§Ø¡:
        1. Elementor JSON structure ÙƒØ§Ù…Ù„Ø©
        2. Sections, Columns, Widgets
        3. Styling (colors, fonts, spacing)
        4. Responsive settings
        
        Ø§Ù„Ù…Ø®Ø±Ø¬Ø§Øª ÙŠØ¬Ø¨ ØªÙƒÙˆÙ† Ù…ØªÙˆØ§ÙÙ‚Ø© 100% Ù…Ø¹ Elementor Pro.`
      }, {
        role: "user",
        content: prompt
      }]
    });
    
    return this.convertToElementorJSON(design);
  }
  
  // 3. ØªØ­ÙˆÙŠÙ„ Ù…Ù† AI Design â†’ Elementor JSON
  convertToElementorJSON(aiDesign: any) {
    return {
      version: "3.0",
      content: [
        {
          elType: "section",
          settings: {
            layout: "boxed",
            background_background: "classic",
            background_color: aiDesign.colors.primary
          },
          elements: [
            {
              elType: "column",
              settings: { _column_size: 100 },
              elements: [
                {
                  elType: "widget",
                  widgetType: "heading",
                  settings: {
                    title: aiDesign.content.heading,
                    typography_typography: "custom",
                    typography_font_family: aiDesign.fonts.heading
                  }
                }
              ]
            }
          ]
        }
      ]
    };
  }
  
  // 4. ØªØµØ¯ÙŠØ± ÙƒÙ€ Elementor Template
  async exportAsElementorTemplate(design: any) {
    const elementorJSON = this.convertToElementorJSON(design);
    
    // Ø­ÙØ¸ ÙƒÙ€ .json file
    const template = {
      content: elementorJSON,
      page_settings: {},
      version: "0.4",
      title: design.title,
      type: "page"
    };
    
    return JSON.stringify(template, null, 2);
  }
}

ğŸ¯ Smart Model Router (Auto-Switch):
class SmartModelRouter {
  async selectModel(request: Request, user: User) {
    // 1ï¸âƒ£ ÙØ­Øµ Free quota Ø£ÙˆÙ„Ø§Ù‹
    if (user.geminiQuota > 0) {
      user.geminiQuota--;
      return {
        model: "gemini-2.0-flash",
        cost: 0,
        message: "ğŸ†“ Using Gemini Flash (Free quota)"
      };
    }
    
    // 2ï¸âƒ£ Auto-switch Ù„Ù€ Groq (Ù…Ø¬Ø§Ù†ÙŠ Ù„Ù„Ø£Ø¨Ø¯)
    if (user.tier === "free") {
      return {
        model: "groq-llama-3.3-70b",
        cost: 0,
        message: "ğŸ†“ Using Groq (Unlimited Free)"
      };
    }
    
    // 3ï¸âƒ£ Ù„Ùˆ Pro â†’ Ø§Ø³ØªØ®Ø¯Ù… Ø§Ù„Ù€ credits
    if (user.tier === "pro" && user.credits > 0) {
      const cost = this.calculateCost(request);
      
      if (user.credits >= cost) {
        user.credits -= cost;
        return {
          model: user.preferredModel || "gpt-4o",
          cost: cost,
          message: `ğŸ’³ Charged $${cost.toFixed(4)} from credits`
        };
      }
    }
    
    // 4ï¸âƒ£ Pay-as-you-go
    if (user.wallet > 0) {
      const cost = this.calculateCost(request);
      
      // Ø¹Ø±Ø¶ Ø§Ù„ØªÙƒÙ„ÙØ© Ù‚Ø¨Ù„ Ø§Ù„ØªÙ†ÙÙŠØ°
      const confirmed = await this.askUserConfirmation(
        `This will cost $${cost.toFixed(4)}. Continue?`
      );
      
      if (confirmed) {
        user.wallet -= cost;
        return {
          model: request.selectedModel,
          cost: cost,
          message: `ğŸ’° Charged $${cost.toFixed(4)} from wallet`
        };
      }
    }
    
    // 5ï¸âƒ£ Fallback â†’ Local (Ollama)
    return {
      model: "ollama-local",
      cost: 0,
      message: "ğŸ  Using Local Model (100% Free & Private)"
    };
  }
  
  calculateCost(request: Request) {
    const pricing = {
      "gpt-4o": 0.0025,
      "claude-sonnet-4.5": 0.003,
      "o3-mini": 0.001,
      "gemini-2.5-pro": 0.002
    };
    
    const tokens = request.estimatedTokens || 1000;
    return (tokens / 1000) * pricing[request.model];
  }
}

class SmartNotificationSystem {
  async notifyUserAboutModelSwitch(from: string, to: string, reason: string) {
    // Toast notification
    toast({
      title: "ğŸ”„ Model switched",
      description: `From ${from} â†’ ${to}\nReason: ${reason}`,
      duration: 5000
    });
    
    // Log in activity feed
    await db.activities.create({
      type: 'model_switch',
      from,
      to,
      reason,
      timestamp: new Date()
    });
  }
  
  async warnAboutQuotaRunningOut(provider: string, remaining: number) {
    if (remaining < 100) {
      toast({
        title: "âš ï¸ Quota running low",
        description: `${provider}: ${remaining} requests left`,
        variant: "warning"
      });
    }
  }
  
  async celebrateSavings(amount: number) {
    toast({
      title: "ğŸ‰ Money saved!",
      description: `You saved $${amount.toFixed(2)} by using free models!`,
      variant: "success"
    });
  }
}

ğŸ“Š Progress Bar Component:
function ModelUsageProgress({ provider }: { provider: QuotaProvider }) {
  const percentage = (provider.used / provider.total) * 100;
  
  return (
    <div className="relative">
      <div className="flex justify-between mb-1">
        <span className="text-sm font-medium">{provider.name}</span>
        <span className="text-sm text-gray-500">
          {provider.used} / {provider.total === Infinity ? 'âˆ' : provider.total}
        </span>
      </div>
      
      <div className="w-full bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-2.5">
        <div 
          className={`h-2.5 rounded-full transition-all duration-500 ${
            percentage > 90 ? 'bg-red-500 animate-pulse' :
            percentage > 70 ? 'bg-yellow-500' :
            'bg-green-500'
          }`}
          style={{ width: `${percentage}%` }}
        />
      </div>
      
      {/* Warning badge */}
      {percentage > 90 && (
        <Badge className="absolute -top-2 -right-2 bg-red-500">
          âš ï¸ Almost full!
        </Badge>
      )}
      
      <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 mt-1">
        Resets: {provider.resetTime}
      </p>
    </div>
  );
}

    return {
      // Ø§Ù„Ø¨ØµÙ…Ø© Ø§Ù„ÙØ±ÙŠØ¯Ø© Ù„Ù„Ø¬Ù‡Ø§Ø²
      browserFingerprint: await this.getBrowserFingerprint(),

        timezone: Intl.DateTimeFormat().resolvedOptions().timeZone,

        // ÙØ­Øµ Ù„Ùˆ ØºÙŠØ± Ø§Ù„Ù€ email
        if (!deviceQuota.emails.includes(user.email)) {
          // ğŸš¨ Suspicious! ÙŠØ­Ø§ÙˆÙ„ ÙŠØ®Ø¯Ø¹ Ø§Ù„Ù†Ø¸Ø§Ù…
          await this.flagSuspiciousActivity(deviceId, user);
          
          return {
            allowed: false,
            reason: "âš ï¸ Free quota already used on this device",
            suggestion: "Upgrade to Pro for unlimited access",
            severity: "high"
          };
        }
        
        return {
          allowed: false,
          reason: "Daily quota finished. Using Groq (unlimited)",
          fallbackModel: "groq"
        };
      }
    }
    
    return { allowed: true };
  }
  
  // 4ï¸âƒ£ Advanced Detection
  async detectAbuse(deviceId: string, user: User) {
    const device = await db.deviceQuotas.findOne({ deviceId });
    
    const redFlags = {
      // ğŸš© Red Flag 1: Multiple emails Ù…Ù† Ù†ÙØ³ Ø§Ù„Ø¬Ù‡Ø§Ø²
      multipleEmails: device.emails.length > 3,
      
      // ğŸš© Red Flag 2: Ø­Ø³Ø§Ø¨Ø§Øª Ø¬Ø¯ÙŠØ¯Ø© ÙƒØªÙŠØ±
      frequentNewAccounts: device.emails.filter(email => {
        const accountAge = this.getAccountAge(email);
        return accountAge < 7; // Ø£Ù‚Ù„ Ù…Ù† Ø£Ø³Ø¨ÙˆØ¹
      }).length > 2,
      
      // ğŸš© Red Flag 3: Ù†ÙØ³ Ø§Ù„Ù€ IP Ø¨Ø­Ø³Ø§Ø¨Ø§Øª ÙƒØªÙŠØ±
      ipAbuse: await this.checkIPAbuse(device.ipAddress),
      
      // ğŸš© Red Flag 4: Usage pattern Ù…Ø´ Ø·Ø¨ÙŠØ¹ÙŠ
      abnormalUsage: this.detectAbnormalPattern(device.usage),
      
      // ğŸš© Red Flag 5: VPN/Proxy detection
      vpnDetected: await this.detectVPN(device.ipAddress)
    };
    
    const abuseScore = Object.values(redFlags).filter(Boolean).length;
    
    if (abuseScore >= 3) {
      await this.handleAbuser(deviceId, user);
      return true;
    }
    
    return false;
  }
  
  // 5ï¸âƒ£ Ø§Ù„ØªØ¹Ø§Ù…Ù„ Ù…Ø¹ Ø§Ù„Ù…Ø®Ø§Ù„ÙÙŠÙ†
  async handleAbuser(deviceId: string, user: User) {
    // Option 1: Soft ban (Ø§Ø³ØªØ®Ø¯Ù… Groq ÙÙ‚Ø·)
    await db.deviceQuotas.update(deviceId, {
      restricted: true,
      allowedModels: ['groq'], // Groq unlimited Ø¨Ø³
      reason: 'Multiple account abuse detected'
    });
    
    // Option 2: CAPTCHA challenge
    await this.requireCAPTCHA(user);
    
    // Option 3: Manual review
    await this.flagForManualReview(deviceId, user);
    
    // Log Ù„Ù„Ù€ admin
    await this.notifyAdmin({
      type: 'abuse_detected',
      deviceId,
      user: user.email,
      severity: 'high',
      details: await this.getAbuseDetails(deviceId)
    });
  }
}

class GenerousQuotaSystem {
  
  // ÙƒÙ„ email = Fresh start!
  async getUserQuota(email: string) {
    // ÙØ­Øµ Ù„Ùˆ Ø§Ù„Ù€ email Ù…ÙˆØ¬ÙˆØ¯
    let user = await db.users.findOne({ email });
    
    if (!user) {
      // Ù…Ø³ØªØ®Ø¯Ù… Ø¬Ø¯ÙŠØ¯ = ÙƒÙ„ Ø§Ù„Ù€ quotas Ù…Ù† Ø£ÙˆÙ„ ÙˆØ¬Ø¯ÙŠØ¯!
      user = await db.users.create({
        email,
        quotas: {
          gemini: { limit: 1500, used: 0, resetDaily: true },
          claude: { limit: 1000, used: 0, resetDaily: true },
          cohere: { limit: 5000, used: 0, resetMonthly: true },
          together: { credits: 25, resetNever: true },
          groq: { limit: Infinity, used: 0 }
        },
        tier: 'free',
        createdAt: new Date()
      });
    }
    
    return user;
  }
  
  // No device fingerprinting!
  // No IP tracking!
  // No abuse detection!
  // Just pure generosity! â¤ï¸
  
  async selectModel(user: User) {
    // Ù†ÙØ³ Ø§Ù„Ù…Ù†Ø·Ù‚ Ø§Ù„Ø°ÙƒÙŠ Ø¨Ø¯ÙˆÙ† Ù‚ÙŠÙˆØ¯
    
    if (user.quotas.gemini.used < user.quotas.gemini.limit) {
      return { model: 'gemini-2.0-flash', cost: 0 };
    }
    
    if (user.quotas.claude.used < user.quotas.claude.limit) {
      return { model: 'claude-3.5-haiku', cost: 0 };
    }
    
    if (user.quotas.cohere.used < user.quotas.cohere.limit) {
      return { model: 'cohere-command-r-plus', cost: 0 };
    }
    
    if (user.quotas.together.credits > 0) {
      return { model: 'together-llama-4', cost: 0.01 };
    }
    
    // Groq forever free!
    return { model: 'groq-llama-3.3-70b', cost: 0 };
  }
}
